Spring and Autumn

Tidbits

— (Yan Xinquan)

If a person who is accustomed to a comfortable life has not encountered suffering, then he will certainly still feel unsatisfied with his comfortable life; but in the eyes of friends whose circumstances are absolutely opposite to his, he feels that being able to reach his level is already a great fortune.

Although soap can be used to wash clothes and remove dirt from the body, if you take a piece of clean white silk cloth, rub it with soap, and put it in the clearest water basin to wash, the clear water will still become turbid. Whose dirt is this, after all?

Mr. Zhu

— Ji'an

Next door to my house, there is a Mr. Zhu, whose words and actions are very peculiar. It is worthwhile to introduce him to the public, to prove that strange people are everywhere in this society.

Mr. Zhu is a normal school graduate. When he first went to work as a teacher, he was like taking office as an official. The clothes he wore were completely new, and the bedding, mosquito nets, etc. were all new. He was originally opposed to wearing leather shoes, but this time he made an exception, spending eight silver dollars to buy a pair of long leather boots with patterned leather in Shanghai. He said, "To be a teacher, you must wear leather shoes, so that you can show off your prestige!" However, he only worked as a teacher for three months before quitting, because a student stole a pencil from him. He felt that the world was going downhill and people's hearts were not as good as before, and that there was nothing to gain from being a teacher.

What did Mr. Zhu do after he lost his job? Others were worried about him, but Mr. Zhu was leisurely and didn't feel anything. He arranged a schedule every day and did his rote work. Last time I went to his house to play, I saw that his schedule was written with: "Get up at 5:00 am every day, practice deep breathing, read scriptures from 7:00 to 10:00, read newspapers from 10:00 to 12:00, take a nap from 1:00 to 3:00, discuss national affairs from 3:00 to 5:00, sit quietly to cultivate one's nature from 7:00 to 9:00..." I couldn't help but laugh secretly when I saw his schedule. I thought: When other people lose their jobs, they go out to find solutions, but he stays at home every day doing boring work. What is his purpose after all?

Recently, my friend said, "Mr. Zhu has become much thinner than before because he is financially strapped after losing his job." However, I thought: Since this is the case, why is he doing boring work at home?

Filial Daughter Cao E

— Qingqu

A few days ago, I saw a news report in the newspaper about "Rebuilding the Caojiang Filial Daughter Temple," saying that it was initiated by the famous Shanghai figure Wang Yiting and others, and it has been three years. Later, due to the poor market, the donations were few, less than 50,000 to 60,000, until August 1st, the main hall was finally able to be raised. It can be seen that the enthusiasm and perseverance of the gentlemen are truly admirable for their belief in the temple.

Cao E was just a daughter. Her father, named Xu, according to his profession, could only "play the rhythm and sing to please the gods," like a descendant of a shaman (see the Preface to the Cao E Stele). It was a very ordinary family background. Unexpectedly, Cao Xu drowned in the water during the ceremony to welcome the wave god at the head of the Qiantang River in May of the second year of Han'an (the reign of Emperor Shun of the Han Dynasty) (the wave god is said to be Wu Zixu, who advised King Fuchai of Wu, was given death, and thrown into the river with a leather bag. Later, a plain carriage and a white horse appeared from time to time, and the Yue people sacrificed to him). At that time, Cao E was only fourteen years old. When she learned of her father's death, she cried day and night by the river, running back and forth, trying to find her father. After seventeen days, she still couldn't find him. Alas! This weak woman jumped into the river, intending to investigate the situation on the spot. Five days later, she really floated up with her father's body in her arms. This shows that although a piece of filial piety cannot escape the myths of the predecessors, from Cao E's own point of view, she is indeed a filial daughter, which everyone can admit!

Therefore, in the past, Du Shang, the magistrate of Shangyu County, had a disciple named Handan Chun, who was still a young man. Du Shang asked Chun to write a Cao E stele inscription, and he immediately wrote it. At first, Wei Lang originally wrote it first, but Wei Lang knew that his writing was not as good as his, and immediately tore up the draft. Later, Cai Yong heard about this and suddenly became curious, thinking that this stele inscription must be read. He rushed there overnight and wrote on the back of the stele: "Yellow silk young woman, grandson pickle mortar," implying the four words "exquisite words." The value of the article can be imagined. In fact, without Cao E's filial piety, the writer's pen could not have achieved this. Now, because it was destroyed by fire seven or eight years ago, enthusiastic gentlemen have collected funds to rebuild it. It can be imagined that the temple will be brand new, and there will be many people who rub and read this stele inscription!

Evening Scene of the Wharf

— Yun Su

The Wai Ma Road in Shanghai's Shiliupu stretches for about a mile, occupied by noisy steamship wharves and warehouses. There, apart from the China Merchants South Station, there are two companies, Ningshao and Dada. Ningshao, in the afternoon when the sun is setting, is like a modern girl, with hundreds of thousands of people rushing into her arms to send寄 things; China Merchants Dada? It is lively from Shenshi to midnight. They are like Lord Mengchang of Qi, embracing the principle of universal rain and dew; along the river wharf, the moon-like electric lights illuminate the rolling long river, shining like ten thousand white snakes. Here, the shouting, the noise, the hawkers' cries, boil into one piece; my return trip is like following the waterway, taking the Xiaochangjiang steamship on the Shanghai-Yangzhou line. These evening scenes can be said to be understood in depth; Dada has been vigorously reformed by the principals in the past two years, and a ticket office has been added. Passengers returning north by boat must first taste the flavor of the window. The shipping company knows that everything is new, and also hangs up neon lights; a heavy streetcar is dragged from afar, and a group of coolies swarm up. This fly-like gathering is a group of porters and footmen; the old Shen Bao, the News, the evening newspaper of the day, and various tabloids are the shouts of old-fashioned newspaper vendors; Suzhou scenery, Wuxi scenery, the low and dumb bamboo pipe songs are the aquatic sideline business of the cultural street book vendors; "Do you want old-brand soap, Guangdong bananas?" These are the food hawkers coming and going; there are also those who do not use sound to represent, and like the cargo Lang Zizi, use响 器 to lure customers. They are the rebels of "one-word hall"! The owner can deceive the sky to bargain, and the buyer can 착地 to return the money; until the tram stops, the night is deep, and the steamship's chimneys emit the roar of lions and tigers! They slowly land, but at this moment, they still want to linger on the edge of the lighter, making a final sale to the customers on the outer舷. The sound of the whistle warns of departure. They drag their heavy footsteps, leaving the wharf, each face with a trace of a smile, indicating that they have made arrangements for tonight's white rice or black rice; at this time, the travelers standing outside the cabin also seem to be murmuring "Farewell Shanghai" in their hearts.

Little Western Paradise

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 17: Don't Ask About a Daughter's Body, It's Hard to Express Hidden Pain; Strive to See the Face of a Noble Person, Admire the Noble Demeanor Together

He walked away congratulating himself like this, but that unfortunate woman kept sending him to the back courtyard to live. After Zhang Jiefu was stunned, he also withdrew and walked towards the house. However, the sound of high heels was the easiest to touch his nerves, so he immediately turned around to greet him. However, he saw that the woman's face was unfamiliar, and there were two bundles of luggage following behind, so he thought that she must be someone related to Commissioner Lan, and he couldn't offend her casually. Therefore, he straightened his face and flashed to the side. The woman said: "Are these the houses here?" He said, revealing a Nanjing accent. Jiefu dared not act rashly, expecting that his guess was right. Just at this time, the accountant in front came in with a roll of red paper and smiled: "Mr. Zhang, didn't you promise to write welcome slogans for us?" Jiefu puffed out his chest and said: "That's my bounden duty. Commissioner Lan, who is coming tomorrow, is our relative." When he said the sentence "is our relative," the voice was very loud. At the same time, he secretly shot his eyes at the woman. Sure enough, the three words "Commissioner Lan" were sent into the woman's ears. The woman seemed to be agitated as well, but Jiefu couldn't look at her too much, so he led the accountant into the house to write slogans. Jiefu was particularly diligent in this matter. He had already poured a bowl of ink, which was neither too thick nor too thin. The table was placed in the middle of the room, with white paper spread on it. Many large and small brushes were opened and placed on the edge of the table, and a large pile of newspapers was piled on the ground, all written with large characters, dripping with ink. (290)

Royal Incense Drifting Record

— Originally Written by Princess Deling of the Qing Dynasty, Translated by Qin Shouou

At that time, those half-open lotus flowers were indeed no longer blooming; they were all quietly waiting; the pink stamens still had not fully emerged.

The rays of the sun leaped over the countless roofs in the capital and shot straight towards the Western Hills. The Summer Palace also passed in its journey; finally, the speed of the sun's rise suddenly increased dramatically, almost jumping up inch by inch, so that it shone all over the lake, making the lake completely coated with a layer of silver.

Now the sun has completely revealed itself in the sky without any concealment!

The spectacle that the Empress Dowager mentioned had finally truly appeared!

At almost the same time, the sun was completely revealed in the sky, and the thousands of buds on the lake surface also all bloomed together; the petals were spread out flat, neatly attached to the green leaves. What surprised me the most was why those half-opened buds were waiting so eagerly before the sun fully emerged, and after the sun was fully hung out, they all bloomed together in an instant; could it be that sunlight has the magic to urge flowers to bloom? The miracles of nature are truly inconceivable.

Lotus flowers are usually mostly pink, and there are also quite a few white ones, but in Kunming Lake, there are quite a few rare species that are not commonly seen outside: on this day, the Empress Dowager was the first to discover two lotus flowers with a slightly green color. She was busy pointing it out to me and quietly told me that this was a famous species of great value. (390)

Social Snapshot

Guest Talk on Official Experience

— Yi Sheng

Wealth can be used to show off, and nobility can easily seek wealth and even more power. Therefore, the children of prominent families all hope that they will become officials in the future! Since the Republic of China, the number of officials has increased day by day, and it is even called the "Republic of Officials." Ordinary people can get half a post, which is a great joy! Therefore, there was a nursery rhyme in the era of the Beijing government: "Generals walk all over the streets, and commanders are as cheap as dogs!" This is similar to the time when An Lushan rebelled in the Tang Dynasty, when all the generals and Jiedushi's certificates were only enough to seek a drunken spree. According to this situation, those who really want to make a living by being officials, wouldn't a part of them become disastrous officials? Or, hanging an official title to scare the common people, otherwise embracing a false name to amuse themselves, it's still okay!

I have a cousin who was originally a writer. It is said that he also used to be an official and held concurrent positions. This makes my humble self considered a relative of an official, and I must have沾得 some official air—although he himself doesn't like others to mention his official affairs! The night before yesterday, we talked about being an official unintentionally. I pestered him to tell me the origin of his official position and the reason why he could be an official without leaving home. He actually agreed to tell me frankly.

"Do you want to know how I got the title of advisor to a certain army in the past? At that time, my friend Lao He—imitating the tone of "My Friend Hu Shih"—was appointed as the minister of a certain department of that army not long ago, and he automatically did me a favor by getting me that title. Although he is a reborn冯妇, he has spent a long time in poverty. We can be considered friends in poverty and lowliness, not only literary friends! That year, he prospered and came to Shanghai. I went to his residence to visit him, and I saw that his demeanor as an official was extraordinary: from afar, guards stood near the corners of the room, arching and guarding him in front and behind. When we sat down casually to chat! I knew about his recent situation, congratulated him, and then hurriedly said goodbye, originally to avoid him suspecting that I had any intention of asking him for something. Not many days later, he was stationed in Suzhou, but he sent a letter of appointment to my home through an organization under his jurisdiction in Shanghai, which was regarded as giving me that official title. I still remember that the servant who delivered the official document was a boy of only thirteen or fourteen with a northern accent, but he had learned some of the etiquette of the officialdom, saying "yes, yes, yes" all the time, and also "congratulations, sir, on your promotion," bowing one after another. His purpose was to get some tips. At that time, I also felt happy in my heart—although that advisor standing in the position of guest minister, his official name did not help with hunger and cold—the friendship of old friends was indeed rich; I gave the boy two dollars at once. He was also content, thanked me a thousand times, and left.

"As for the position of special commissioner of a certain provincial government in Shanghai, it came from a classmate surnamed Wu who exchanged Worcester porcelain with me. At that time, he was acting as the acting secretary-general of the provincial government due to special opportunities. I think he valued our past mutual friendship and recommended me to the acting chairman, almost saying that I was no less than Wolong and Fengchu—according to what he said in his letter—as a result, he attached the provincial government's commission to his private letter and sent it to me. The commission also had the words 'approved monthly allowance of one hundred yuan for a carriage and horse.' This was a paid position, because the province had not been established for long and was located in a remote border area. The provincial government wanted me to do propaganda work and handle official affairs in Beijing and Shanghai. After two months, I finally did some written work, but as for the salary with the beautiful name of夫马费, I repeatedly asked Wu Jun to collect it and remit it, but there was always only a wild goose going but no return. Soon, the political situation in the province changed, and my title of special commissioner was not added to by the successor, so it was listed in the 'human evolution and elimination.'

"These two official positions that didn't require me to go out also gave me a practical experience of a common saying, which is 'Don't be an official if you don't have anyone in the court'! What's the point of talking about it? An official like this with the nature of a bad check, how can it be loaded by cars and斗 in this Republic of China? Isn't that just making a mess?"

After hearing this, I couldn't help but feel that my cousin's official position was just like a small bubble disappearing with the political tide that pushed the front waves behind. The daily newspaper that I read during the day was placed in front of me, and in my hallucination, I seemed to vaguely hear the sound of the surging new tide coming from the folds of the newspaper.

Sports News

Satisfactory Outcome of Charity Tennis Tournament: Xu Chengji Defeats Lin Baohua, Qiu Feihai Loses to Carlsen Two Sets to None, Xu and Lin Win Doubles in a Thrilling Match, Xu Chengji Departs Shanghai This Morning to Return to Java, Ticket Sales Exceed 4,000 Yuan

The grand charity tennis tournament, initiated enthusiastically by Bureau Chief Wu Xingya and gentlemen Tan Jingsun and Lin Fang, with fervent support from all sectors, was held yesterday afternoon at the Chinese Tennis Club on Singapore Road. The outcome was exceptionally satisfactory. Approximately over a thousand spectators were in attendance. It is reported that ticket sales reached a considerable sum of four to five thousand yuan, which will be announced by the initiators in the coming days. As for the competition results, the most attention-grabbing was the first singles match, where Xu Chengji defeated Lin Baohua two sets to one: 4-6, 6-4, 6-3. Qiu Feihai lost to Carlsen two sets to none: 6-2, 6-2. The final, thrilling doubles match saw Xu Chengji and Lin Baohua win two sets to one against Carlsen and Dofu: 6-3, 4-6, 6-2. The performance concluded close to nightfall, with Madam Wu Xingya presenting awards, gifting each performing athlete with a large silver cup. Xu Chengji, eager to return home, decided to depart Shanghai this morning to return south.

Xu Defeats Lin Baohua: Xu Chengji 4-6, 6-4, 6-3, Lin Baohua

Consecutive Intense Battles Diminish Chengji's Performance: The previous day, play was halted due to rain. Xu had previously led Lin Baohua by a score of four games to zero. Because it was an exhibition and the weather was inclement, the previous score was not continued, and a new match was played. However, due to consecutive days of intense matches, Xu was noticeably fatigued. Therefore, his performance against Lin Baohua yesterday was significantly diminished. Although he emerged victorious, there were many close calls. Lin Baohua's performance was quite exceptional, truly "defeated but still impressive."

Lin Puts Forth All His Effort to Take the First Set: Lin Baohua approached yesterday's match against Xu Chengji with a do-or-die spirit. His half-court chops and powerful forehand drives put Xu Chengji in a desperate situation. Xu's serves yesterday were rarely good, and his drives lacked precision. Countless balls went out of bounds. Xu served first, losing the first two games. In the third game, Lin broke Xu's serve and surged ahead, winning four consecutive games. His subtle and flanking chops repeatedly defeated Xu, resulting in a score of 4-2. Many of Xu's forehand drives went out of bounds. Lin led 5-3. In the tenth game, with Lin serving, at 30-30, Xu inexplicably sent an easy volley into the net. Subsequently, Lin sent a high ball, which Xu mistakenly judged as out of bounds, thus losing the first set 6-4.

Xu Chengji Retakes the Second Set: In the second set, Lin showed signs of fatigue after the intense battle of the first set. Xu remained remarkably calm, unhurriedly taking a 3-1 lead. However, due to numerous mistakes on both sides, the excitement of the match was greatly diminished. Lin, dissatisfied with a linesman's call, readily conceded the eighth game. Xu took a 5-3 lead and then won the second set 6-4. In this set, Xu began to anticipate Lin's chops and quickly responded, but his saves were still few and far between.

The Third Set Ends in Thrilling Fashion: Although the situation was very tense, Xu Chengji's victory seemed more assured, as Xu did not appear strained or exhausted, remaining remarkably calm. In the fourth game, due to Lin's double fault and a net touch on his serve, Xu took a 3-1 lead. However, in the next game, Xu unexpectedly lost his serve. After 3-3, Xu quickly won two more games, taking a 5-3 lead. In the ninth game, with Xu serving, he trailed 30-40, a perilous situation. In the next game, Lin was poised to make it 5-5, but unexpectedly, one of Xu's shots grazed the net and dropped over, leaving Lin, though at the net, helpless. After deuce, Xu won two more points in a row, winning the third set 6-3.

Photograph of Xu Chengji and Lin Baohua (Taken by Qichang)

Qiu Feihai Loses to Carlsen: Carlsen 6-2, 6-2, Qiu Feihai

Old Qiu is Helplessly Decrepit: Carlsen and Qiu Feihai took the court next. Qiu had previously lost to Xu Chengji 7-5, 6-1, so yesterday's loss was also expected. Old Qiu is now old and past his prime. Against Carlsen, he had no chance of survival, unable to defend or attack. His only cross-court drive was also ineffective. Carlsen's serve speed, net coverage, and powerful smashes were superior to Qiu in every aspect. Qiu won one game in the first set. After 4-1, he won another game. The set ended 6-2. In the second set, after 3-0 and 4-1, each won one game. It also ended 6-2.

Doubles Exhibition Full of Thrills: Xu Chengji and Lin Baohua 6-3, 4-6, 6-2, Carlsen and Dofu

Xu Chengji's Performance is Divine: Xu Chengji did not fully display his skills in the singles match. However, when he took the court for the doubles match, his performance was simply divine and flawless. Lin Baohua was overshadowed. Moreover, the opponents were also skilled doubles players, making the doubles match full of thrills, with only Dofu being slightly weaker. Xu's serve, net play, and especially his powerful smashes from the baseline were rarely seen by Shanghai residents. If Xu and Lin worked together and trained, they would be a formidable doubles team. In the first set, both opened with a service win, but Dofu did not win his serve in the fourth game, allowing Xu and Lin to take a 3-1 lead. Each added two more games, making it 5-3. Xu served, winning the first set 6-3. In the second set, Carlsen's serve failed, making it 4-2. However, Xu and Lin also failed on their serves. A game that could have been won was instead won by the opponents, who won four games in a row, taking it 6-4, making it one set apiece. In the third set, Xu and Lin continued their efforts, winning 5-1 and then 6-2 to win.

Xu Chengji Scheduled to Leave Shanghai This Morning

Unfavorable Weather, Unsuitable for Flying: After the match, Mr. Sun Linfang delivered a speech, thanking everyone for their enthusiastic support and expressing gratitude on behalf of the disaster victims. He then presented each performing player with a silver cup as a memento. Madam Wu Xingya presented the awards. As for Xu Chengji, yesterday he was repeatedly persuaded by Tan Jing, Chen Qihao, and Yin Dong to stay longer and give more performances to repay the Shanghai people for their warm welcome. Chen Qijun was entrusted to inquire about airline information in order to fly south and avoid missing his ship. According to Mr. Chen, the previous passenger plane encountered wind along the way and was delayed for a long time. Given the windy conditions, flying was not advisable. The previous plan had to be abandoned. Xu, eager to return home, was difficult to keep. He is scheduled to take the Zinega of the Java Company at eight o'clock this morning, returning directly to Java. He may disembark for performances during the stopover in Hong Kong.

Municipal Education Bureau Stipulates: Qualifications for Athletes in Various Schools

Bureau Affairs Meeting Decides on Five Measures, Notifying All Middle and Elementary Schools to Comply

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued an order to all public and private middle and elementary schools in the city stating that the qualifications for athletes in the joint middle and elementary school sports meets held by the bureau in the past have yet to be stipulated, often leading to disputes. The measures for stipulating the qualifications for these athletes have been submitted to the 302nd Bureau Affairs Meeting for discussion and have been recorded in the minutes after a resolution. The measures are hereby issued, ordering all schools to comply. The measures for stipulating the qualifications for athletes are as follows: (1) School athletes must have studied at their respective schools for at least one semester to participate. (2) Students must have passing grades in both academics and conduct to participate. (3) Students who have studied at School A, transferred to School B midway, and then returned to School A to study, but have not yet completed one semester, may not participate. (4) School graduates, graduates of continuing education, and students who are not students of the school may not represent the school. (5) All participating athletes must provide photos to the committee for verification. Impersonation is prohibited. Violators will be subject to disciplinary action by the principal and physical education instructor.

Donghua and Others Submit to National Games: Requesting Inclusion of Small Ball as an Exhibition Event

Since the establishment of the Shanghai Small Ball Association, the formerly neglected small ball sport has attracted public attention. The contents of the petition are copied below: Petition to support the Shanghai Small Ball Association's request to include small ball sports as an exhibition event in the National Games: Small soccer is a sport that has recently emerged as a distinct discipline. This sport offers the interest of soccer without its intensity and is simple to set up and economical in time, achieving both objectives. As such, it has quickly gained popularity throughout Shanghai. At the Shanghai Municipal No. 1 Public Sports Field, the small soccer competition had over 200 participating teams. The Shanghai West Small Soccer Competition Association (Qunhua Qiangguang, etc.) had over 300. The Shanghai East Competition (Pudong Youth Association Simple Sports Field, etc.) also had over 100 teams. Numerous other cup competitions have been held. It is estimated that there are over a thousand small ball organizations in Shanghai, indicating that this sport requires immediate attention and promotion. This time, the association is petitioning your committee to select the best players from this city to participate in the National Games exhibition. We are deeply moved by this and express our sympathy. We dare to jointly request that your committee approve the association's request to include small ball sports as an exhibition event in the National Games, in order to promote this sport and fulfill the public's expectations. We respectfully submit this petition to the Preparatory Committee of the Sixth National Games.

Parents' Association Organization

--Outline

(Nanjing, 14th): The National Children's Year Implementation Committee announced the full text of the Parents' Association organization outline on the 14th, totaling eleven key points: (1) The purpose is to cultivate parents' wisdom and virtue, research and implement methods of child rearing, and increase children's happiness. (2) Parents' associations should be established extensively in various localities. (3) Research and implementation items: (A) Hold parent-teacher conferences, lectures, and discussion meetings, etc.; (B) Liaise with schools and families to promote the effectiveness of children's education, etc.

County Junior High School Principal Removed and Replaced

The principal of Shanghai County Junior High School and Rural Normal School, Fan Chongheng, was ordered by the Jiangsu Education Department to be replaced. According to a report from the provincial inspector, the school's performance was poor during his inspection. The principal has been in charge for two years, and the results are unsatisfactory. He should no longer act as the principal. The county is instructed to select qualified personnel to submit for approval and appointment in order to fundamentally reorganize and effectively rectify the situation. The County Education Bureau was instructed to select Liao Jianmin, a graduate of the Political Science Department of Central University, to take over the position. The county submitted the nomination for approval, and the department has approved the request and instructed the Education Bureau to inform the officer to report to the school for duty.

Chinese Institute of Engineers Unveils Zhu Mother Memorial Scholarship Winners: Lin Tongyan and Wu Huaqing Selected

In memory of his mother, Madam Gu, Mr. Zhu Qiqing, a member of the Chinese Institute of Engineers, donated one thousand yuan to the institute to establish the Zhu Mother Memorial Scholarship. The annual interest of one hundred yuan will be awarded to Chinese scholars who have made outstanding achievements and demonstrated a special interest in research on any engineering academic subject and have written papers on it. The award is given annually to one winner, and the award is presented at the opening of each annual meeting after the winner is selected. This year, nine papers were submitted. Xu Mingcai, Zhang Gongjiu, Li Qianruo, Qiu Weiyu, and Ma Deji were appointed as the judging committee. The received papers are listed below: 1. Wu Xu, "Wireless Radio Control Technology and Application," 2. Li Rui and Zhou Houkun, "Electric Indicator for Ship Rudder Position," 3. Zhang Shiming, "The Law of Swinging and Reciprocating Motion," 4. Li Fen, "Research on Earthwork Calculation Problems," 5. Li Fuguo, "Graphical Method for Highway Alignment," 6. Lin Tongyan, "Direct Force Rate Distribution Method," 7. Jiang Yu, "Discussion on the Design and Economy of Plate Arch Bridges," 8. Wu Huaqing, "Paper Models and Architecture," 9. C. A. Middleton South: "Analysis Ground Earth used for Dumping Purposes." After evaluation by the judging committee, the Zhu Mother Memorial Scholarship for the 24th year should be awarded to Mr. Lin Tongyan and Mr. Wu Huaqing. According to the charter, each will be awarded one hundred yuan. Because no one was selected last year, two awards are given this year. The scholarship was awarded at the annual meeting held in Nanning on August 12th of this year.

Columbia University Faculty Study Group Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday

Visited the city center and educational institutions yesterday; free visits today; mayor's banquet tomorrow afternoon

The faculty study group from the Teachers College of Columbia University's Institute of Family Education, who came to China for a study tour, arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning at 7:15 a.m. on the Beijing-Shanghai overnight express train, having traveled south from Tianjin and Beijing via the capital. The group will study in Shanghai for three days and then return to their country by ship. Details are noted below:

Arrival in Shanghai: The group of Chinese and Americans came to China to first study family education in the North China region of Tianjin and Beijing. They then traveled south by Tianjin-Pukou Railway and arrived in the capital a few days ago. They left Beijing on the overnight express train last night at 11:00 p.m. and arrived at the North Station at 7:15 a.m. this morning. The municipal government specially sent Secretary Zhang Tingrong and Lin Yannan, and the Education Bureau sent Commissioner Tang Jinbo and Shen Jiahe, Ms. Qi, and others to welcome them. The group arrived in Shanghai and stayed at Room 842, 8th Floor, New Asia Hotel, Yangbei Sichuan Road.

Members: A total of ten people came to China this time, led by Professor Benjamin R. Andrews of the Department of Home Economics at Columbia University. He is an authority on family education in the United States, has authored many books, and currently serves as the chairman of the National Committee on Home Affairs and the editor of the Lippincott Home Economics Series. In addition to Professor Andrews' wife and son, Little Andrews, the other seven teachers accompanying him are Bessie Pearl, Mawahna Pease, Patricia Olga Kelly, Ruth Nelson, Susanna Jenny, and Vivi.

Visits: Departing at 9:30 a.m. yesterday, they visited the Food and Nutrition Institute on Avenue Edward VII, then went to Jiaotong University in Xujiahui, and then toured the City God Temple. At 11:30 a.m., accompanied by Ms. Shen Jiahe of the Education Bureau, they toured the city center and visited the new municipal government building, where they were received by Mayor Wu. At 12:30 p.m., the National Young Men's Christian Association hosted a banquet at the New Asia Hotel. From 4:00 p.m. to 6:00 p.m., they had a tea party at the Young Women's Christian Association, exchanging views and giving speeches with Ms. Wang Guoxiu, Zhang Xiaomei, Liu Wang Liming, Deng Yuzhi, Zhu Juebao, Peng Wangquan, and other ladies.

Banquet: The group is scheduled for free visits today. Tomorrow morning, Dr. Sanmei will host a breakfast. At 9:00 a.m., they will go to Dachang to visit the Rural College. At 11:00 a.m., the National Young Men's Christian Association will listen to Tao Xingzhi's speech on "Popular Education." At 12:30 p.m., Mayor Wu will host a lunch at his private residence on Haig Road. At 2:30 p.m., they will go to Jiangwan Yeyuan to visit the Pulmonary Sanatorium. They will leave Shanghai on the President Hoover that evening to return to the United States.

Little Men (10) (4)

— Original work by American author Louisa May Alcott, translated by Zheng Xiaocang (Zonghai)

The water play was suddenly followed by a flurry of pillows flying chaotically in the air. Many little white-clad spirits emerged from their beds with a clamor, throwing these pillows. This war broke out in several rooms, along the upstairs corridor, and sometimes even spread to the nursery, as the pursued warriors sometimes retreated here. Strangely, it seemed that no one cared or even minded about this kind of outburst; no one tried to stop it or showed any surprise. Nansui kept hanging up many hands without interruption, and Mrs. Pei kept searching for clean clothes, acting as if nothing had been disturbed at all. No, she even joined in herself, chasing a reckless child out of the room and throwing back at him the pillow he had thrown at her.

"Aren't they going to get hurt?" Ned asked, watching drowsily, laughing uncontrollably.

"Oh, no! We allow a pillow fight every Saturday night. The pillowcases will be changed tomorrow anyway; and after the children's baths, it helps their blood circulate and gives them a little more warmth; so I quite like it myself," Mrs. Pei said, while busily sorting out a dozen socks.

"What an extremely lovely school!" Ned exclaimed in admiration.

"This is a strange school," Mrs. Pei said with a smile; "you must know that we don't believe in too many rules or too much homework, just to make the children suffer. At first, I forbade them to get up in their pajamas and make trouble; but, thank you, that was completely useless. They are just like puppets in a toy box, as soon as they are put in, they will kneel up again. So I made a deal with them: I allow them fifteen minutes of 'pillow fight' every Saturday night; they promise to go to sleep quietly on the other nights. I tried it, and it worked. If they don't keep their promise, they don't get to play; if they do keep it, I hide away the glassware and put the lamps in a safe place, and just let them make a big fuss as they please."

"This is a wonderful plan," Ned said, feeling that he would like to join in this chaos, but not daring to make such a request on the first night. So he just fell asleep admiring the scene—it was indeed a lively scene.

Yarn and Cotton: Exchange Rate Adjustment Reduces Margin, Prices Soar, Bullish Sentiment Rises in Yarn Market

The yarn market continued to rise, and the situation was particularly strong. Because the exchange rate tended to shrink and the margin increased, rumors arose again in the market, and the old story of inflation was brought up again. This was actually because general speculators and industry insiders saw that many yarn mills were closed, and they were very enthusiastic about going long on cotton yarn. When the price fell, people bought, and as the trading floor tightened, the market rose. However, the environment was still poor, and current yarn sales were bleak, and all parties were still restricted by finance.

Golden Rooster Soars by Two Yuan

At the opening of the pre-market trading in spot yarn, the prices of all months rose uniformly, and the momentum was quite tight. Because the margin increased, the market was full of rumors, and shorts were covering their positions. However, the overseas cotton market was still weak, and second-grade yarn fell by more than two yuan. Local buying interest was still strong. As a result, the prices of all months rose by one yuan to one yuan and three, five, eight jiao compared with the closing price of the previous day. At the opening of the afternoon session, buying became more intense, and people's minds were tense, saying that the off-exchange trading after the margin closed had exceeded 923 or 924 yuan. Therefore, buyers gathered and came in, and the pace became tighter and tighter. However, when the market was about to close, Da Fu took profits, and the market price rebounded slightly. World Cotton Markets Fall Across the Board

Yesterday, American cotton opened, and prices for all months fell by five to eight points. The market price in the early morning was weak due to bad news from Liverpool, selling by foreign merchants, and profit-taking by bulls. It then stabilized slightly due to buying by fellow traders and short covering. In the afternoon, New Orleans, local gangs, Wall Street, cotton farmers, and the public all sold, and the market fell again. Weather reports indicated that the southwestern cotton area had turned cool and rainy, and hedging increased, which was the main reason for the market's instability. Unfortunately, the lending problem often prevented sellers from selling large amounts. As a result, spot prices fell by 15 points, and futures prices fell by 14 to 18 points. English cotton spot prices fell by 7 points, and futures prices fell by 3 to 5 points. When Indian cotton was at a low price, European exporters bought slightly, and shorts also covered their positions. There were not many sellers, and the market was stable. It is estimated that Pingguoer fell by 0.75 rupees, Oumula fell by 0.25 rupees, and Bailuoxi fell by 0.375 to 0.5 rupees. The original telegram is recorded on the left (dated the 13th):

In addition, the price of foreign wheat was difficult to determine for a while, and the price of domestic wheat was also seen as expensive, so it was stable in the midst of weakness. By the afternoon sessions, the market gradually stabilized because the price of gold rose sharply, and it was rumored that the banking industry was still looking for continued highs. Outside bulls continued to absorb smoothly. Although some large factories sold off, the market was as stable as usual. It was rumored that talk of currency circulation had started again in the market, and future ups and downs were inevitably related. As a result, this month was up by a small two and a half li, September was up by two and a half li, October was up by two and a half li, and November and December were up by two and a half li.

Wheat Market Rose in the Afternoon

Yesterday's wheat market opened in the morning, and the prices for all months were generally flat and weak. Because the quoted price for foreign wheat fell slightly by one or two jiao, the asking price for each month was also slightly lower than the previous day by one or two fen. Trading in each session was also light. Until the afternoon session opened, the market rose step by step again. Because the price of gold rebounded, the current asking price for foreign wheat was around five yuan, and the price of wheat in the mainland was still holding up, not softening with the Shanghai market, so trading turned strong and the market was good. Observing the later steps, it will present a situation of long-term strength and short-term weakness. As a result, this month rose by three fen, September rose by four fen, October rose by five fen, November rose by two fen, and December rose by three fen. The current wheat market yesterday again refused to open because the factory was thinking of pressing the price down by a few fen before showing intention to buy. Customers in the mainland were unwilling to let go, so there were no only bags seen delivered.

Shen Bao National Goods Weekly

Contributions

Two Knives and a Pair of Pliers

— Yang An

Who has the greatest power to promote national goods? I say it is the people who hold two knives and a pair of pliers.

The first knife is the tailor who uses scissors. For example, one day the tailors get together for a large meeting and decide on a trade agreement saying: "From now on, we will refuse to make any clothes from non-national goods fabrics." In this way, no matter how trendy and fashionable the young masters and ladies are, they cannot but submit to the scissors of the head tailor. Perhaps the great success of national goods comes from the hands of tailors. It is said that in some places, many tailors have already implemented this, and when they encounter a Westernized young master or a modern woman entrusting them to make clothes from foreign fabrics, although they do not necessarily refuse, they always announce that Madam So-and-so or Miss So-and-so from the So-and-so household does not use national goods but uses foreign goods. In this way, everyone is somewhat wary, thinking that it is somewhat scary for people with scissors to have patriotism.

The second knife is the friend who cuts paper and sharpens pencils. If they are determined not to cut foreign paper and not to sharpen foreign pencils when using a knife to cut paper or sharpen a pencil, then at least China's stationery industry can improve somewhat, and the paper mills that are about to close may not be without a solution. This knife should also be used with caution.

The third friend holding pliers to open soda, orange juice, beer, etc., please be silent for half a minute before opening the bottle and look at the trademark on the bottle to see if it is a national good or not. If it is not a national beverage, I advise you not to easily open this bottle cap. In particular, those who are doctors and waiters should not let small copper coins block their hearts and act like crazy people, opening and pouring all kinds of foreign soda and beer to act as salesmen for foreign merchants. Master Yiyiguan

Saving the Country Should Start with Oneself

— Master Qiaqiaguan

Mr. Gu Shilin said: "Everyone is responsible for the rise and fall of the world." Today, our country is suffering from both internal and external troubles, and the pressure is on each other. Natural disasters and man-made disasters occur frequently year after year. If we let this situation continue, the country will surely perish! As a national, how can we sit idly by and not save it?

But, "Save the country!" "Save the country!" You advise me to save the country, and I also advise you to save the country. Everyone only knows how to focus on others saving the country, and does not know how to focus on themselves saving the country. This kind of "saving the country" will only result in you deceiving me and me deceiving you. "Saving the country" may also turn into "destroying the country"!

Now, let's not talk about anything else, let's just talk about the matter of "saving the country with national goods." Ah! Everyone must promote "national goods"! The reason why the country has become so poor and weak is because everyone does not know how to promote "national goods"! Therefore, you advise me to promote "saving the country with national goods," and I also encourage you to promote "saving the country with national goods." But in reality, does everyone really promote "saving the country with national goods"? No, everyone is promoting "destroying the country with foreign goods." Friends, don't blame me for saying this too harshly. Facts tell us that this is indeed the case! If you don't believe me, then please take the time to check the old accounts of the past two years - "National Goods Year" and "Women's National Goods Year" - and see what the results are. Alas! Isn't the "import surplus" of "foreign goods" increasing rather than decreasing? The "import surplus" of "foreign goods" continues to increase. The more it makes the whole of China lifeless! Everywhere you only hear about "bankruptcy" and "economic downturn." Thinking about it carefully, this is really because everyone is not sincere in saving the country. On the surface, it is you advising me and me advising you. In reality, it is just mutual deception and mutual use! If this continues, wouldn't "saving the country" also turn into "destroying the country"?

Therefore, my humble opinion is that "saving the country should start with oneself." In other words, for the current plan, the only way is for everyone to strive for themselves, so that we can save the country. "Saving the country with national goods" is also the same. There is no need to focus solely on others, and you cannot solely supervise others. As long as you can sincerely save the country and seriously promote "national goods," that's fine. If everyone is like this, then the goal of "saving the country with national goods" will eventually be achieved one day. Otherwise, it's just talk. Now that this "Student National Goods Year" is almost three-quarters over. So, with this remaining quarter of a year, I hope everyone will use the spirit of "saving the country should start with oneself" and step up their self-efforts!

Believe it or Not!

— Lu Xiangxian

Nowadays, nine out of ten middle school students use fountain pens to write letters.

Taking schools as a unit, the percentage of students wearing imported Western suits is 3% in elementary schools, 10% in middle schools, and more than 60% in universities. But university students are the most outstanding young people in China.

Long gowns made of indanthrene cloth have recently become increasingly popular, with elementary school students and middle school students wearing them the most.

The belts that students like to wear the most mostly come from Hong Kong, but they are sold by national goods companies.

Go to the school dormitory to take a look, and of the ink bottles placed on the desks, one-tenth are Waterman, three-tenths are Carter, two-tenths are Minsheng and Butterfly brand and others. Remember! This year is Student National Goods Year! Baling

Two Things Worth Celebrating

— Ba Ling

"Promoting domestic goods is a permanent endeavor, not something confined to a specific year or time. We should always keep the promotion of domestic goods in mind, no matter when or where we are. Whenever an opportunity arises, we should find ways to promote it, so that our country's domestic goods movement can achieve good results and great achievements under our efforts." These are words that I, as a reporter, often share with friends who are passionate about the domestic goods movement.

Recently, I have discovered two things in our Republic of China's domestic goods movement that are worth celebrating and deserve to be highlighted here. I am writing them down now to show that our country's domestic goods movement, after some time of effort and promotion by many people, has indeed achieved considerable results.

The first thing is the reduction of import surplus. According to the report of the International Trade Weekly of the International Trade Bureau, the total value of foreign goods imported into our country in the first half of the year was 545,455,295 yuan, and the total value of exports was 259,369,672 yuan. As a result, the import surplus was 286,085,623 yuan. In the same period last year, the import value was 569,849,836 yuan, the export value was 268,544,717 yuan, and the total import surplus was 301,300,5123 yuan. Comparing the first half of last year with the first half of this year, the import surplus has decreased by 15,219,500 yuan in the first half of this year. Isn't this something worth celebrating? It shows that promoting domestic goods, as long as we continue to work hard, can definitely achieve results. Mr. Pan Yangyao said: "We must contribute our share to the promotion of domestic goods, no matter how small. Doing something is always better than doing nothing." These words have great significance. From now on, I hope everyone will be determined to work hard and diligently to do more for the domestic goods movement. Then, when the statistics are compiled next year, there will definitely be good results to reveal to us.

The second thing is the great unity of domestic cigarette companies. We know that the unity of domestic industry peers is a very effective and powerful organization. The worst thing is competition among peers, mutual killing among peers. Tianxu Wosheng said: "Competition among peers is the death certificate of the domestic goods business." This sentence is very reasonable. Now the domestic cigarette industry is the first to wake up, which is really a good phenomenon and a good organization. From now on, I believe that the domestic cigarette industry will have considerable development and extraordinary progress. I hope that the unity of the domestic cigarette industry will influence other domestic goods businesses to continue to unite, jointly discuss the standards of products, discuss marketing channels, study the improvement of goods, and set consistent prices. If all these things can be done step by step, how can the domestic goods business fail to stand firm? Therefore, on the one hand, I express my great approval of the unity of the domestic cigarette industry. At the same time, I especially hope that other industries will also unite and stand on the same front, working hard and fighting for the domestic goods business. That is what I hope for twelve thousand times.

Writing in a rambling way, I have already taken up a lot of space. I am very sorry. Finally, I sincerely pray that my hopes will not become illusions and that there will always be a factual manifestation.

Written for the Aspiring Students

— Meng Zhao

Time flies like a galloping horse! In the blink of an eye, summer vacation has arrived again! Aspiring students, happily returning home, what work will you do during this summer vacation? I, the writer, am not talented, but may I humbly offer some suggestions for the students?

This year "is the Student Domestic Goods Year." As the name suggests, have students made efforts for the domestic goods movement? This is something that should be reflected upon. More than half of the Student Domestic Goods Year has passed! So, during this summer vacation, we should do more work to promote domestic goods. My humble opinion is as follows:

(1) Compile a Domestic Goods Survey Form

The things we need in our daily lives, such as food, supplies, and clothing, are all available as domestic goods, and some are even better than imported goods. However, while we have a deep impression of the famous domestic goods, there are so many other names that we can't remember them all! Therefore, compiling a domestic goods survey form is extremely urgent! Such as the place of origin of domestic goods, production status, supply and demand situation, comparison of advantages and disadvantages, comparison of prices, reasons why Chinese people like to use them or not... In short, the more detailed the better.

(2) Urge Parents to Buy Domestic Goods: A General Mobilization Your fathers, mothers, sisters, uncles, aunts, etc. If you find them fond of buying imported goods, you should gently explain the benefits of using domestic goods. If it doesn't work after repeated attempts, you might as well resort to "military persuasion." The so-called "military persuasion" is to smash the foreign goods! After smashing them, if you are beaten or scolded, you can then persuade them while crying. No parent will not be moved and follow your good advice!

(3) Organize a Summer Student Consumer Cooperative Students in each region and from the same hometown should unite, regardless of their schools (different schools), and use their saved pocket money to form a small capital and organize a "Summer Student Consumer Cooperative." For each individual's self-study supplies and the stationery, books, brushes, ink, etc. needed after the start of school, purchase them wholesale from domestic goods companies in bulk. This not only saves the high cost of buying retail, but also allows you to practice business experience. Be sure to choose an older, capable, and honest leader. Female students may also participate, because women are more meticulous and patient in internal affairs than men. "Studying without forgetting the domestic goods movement" can indeed be realized! Students can also work hard to pay attention to the import surplus situation in the customs trade booklets, comparative charts of people's love for domestic goods in various countries around the world, and various statistics on domestic goods! I look forward to amazing results!

Improving Silk Cotton Manufacturing Methods

— Tianxu Wosheng

Silk cotton is a rich product of Zhejiang Province. Its effect of keeping out the cold is light and warm, and the price is also very cheap, which is better than wool and leather goods. However, it is a pity that the manufacturing method is not good, and it often exudes oil and turns yellow over time, resulting in a drop in selling price. The Haining Silk Cotton Factory therefore sent a letter to the Machine Association, asking Tianchu Wosheng to find a way to solve this problem. After many trials, it was indeed successful. Every catty of silk cotton has its silkworm pupa oil removed during manufacturing, and it is bleached. The cost is less than a dime, and it will never change color. It can also increase toughness and luster. Because I think that most women in the countryside stick to the old methods and do not know how to improve them, once they turn yellow, it is a lot of trouble to try to salvage them. Therefore, it is advisable to do it while it is still wet at the beginning of manufacturing, so that the finished products can be uniform. Therefore, it is specially made public as follows for those with knowledge to spread and adopt.

The equipment and procedures used are all in accordance with ordinary methods, that is, the cocoons are boiled in soup, and then boiled with alkali as usual. After peeling out the silkworm pupae, each five liang is made into a sheet, and each twenty sheets is made into a skein. Each six skeins are soaked in a one-dou crock. The original amount of water in the half-lead bucket was about fifteen catties. Now, the following medicines should be added to this water:

(Alkali Substitute) Use eight taels of anhydrous sodium carbonate for each batch, first dissolve it in fifteen catties of water, then add four taels of light calcium hydroxide, heat to boil, let it stand until it settles, and then take the clear liquid to soak six skeins of silk cotton for about four hours. Take it out and rinse it with cold water to start bleaching. If you don't bleach it immediately, it's okay to soak it in clean water for a long time. The above is a self-made "caustic soda solution", which saves 70% compared to using caustic soda. The purpose is to combine the pupa oil contained in it with alkali to form soap, so it can be washed away and not left in the silk cotton, so that it will oxidize, turn yellow, and smell. Then carry out acid bleaching as follows:

(Bleaching Agent) Use eight taels of "anhydrous sodium sulfite" for each batch and dissolve it in fifteen catties of water to become solution A. Separately, use four taels of hydrochloric acid with a specific gravity of 20 degrees and dissolve it in fifteen catties of water to become solution B. You can use a beaker to measure 160 cc (equal to four Chinese taels). Soak the bleached silk cotton that has been alkalized and degreased in solution A first, take it out and wring it dry after five minutes, then move it to solution B and soak it for five minutes, take it out and wring it dry, and then rinse it with clean water. Then, dry it in the usual way, and it will become pure white silk cotton without flaws.

After using the above bleaching agent once, just add four taels of "anhydrous sodium sulfite" to solution A and eighty cc of "20-degree hydrochloric acid" to solution B, and add water to make up the original amount. You can use it again without discarding it. Therefore, the actual consumption is only half each time. Moreover, it does not take much time and effort. Anyone who uses the old method to make silk cotton can improve it in this way.

The chemicals used are already produced in our province, but you need to buy them in bulk to get a good price; buying pounds retail is quite expensive. If you calculate according to the chemical reagent price list of the Instrument Museum, anhydrous sodium carbonate and sodium sulfite are both one yuan per pound, and 20-degree hydrochloric acid costs half a yuan per pound. Therefore, if you do a small test to see the effect, it doesn't matter if it's expensive. If you are manufacturing in large quantities, you should use 2,000 catties of silk cotton as a unit and purchase a box of anhydrous sodium sulfite, which costs 58 yuan, two boxes of 20-degree sulfuric acid, which cost 14 yuan and 40 cents, and four and a half dan of anhydrous sodium carbonate (pure alkali), which costs about 32 yuan, for a total of 104 yuan and 40 cents, plus about 110 yuan for loading and transportation, etc. The chemicals used per catty of silk cotton cost less than six cents. As for light calcium hydroxide, which is hydrated lime, you can buy quicklime locally, add 40 catties of water to every 100 catties of quicklime, sprinkle it to make it disintegrate into powder, and then sift it before use.

The Shame of Students

— Wei Yuan

This year is called the Student Domestic Goods Year. This does not mean that only students should try their best to purchase domestic goods this year, while other people can be more casual. In fact, all citizens should try their best to purchase domestic goods. The reason why this year can be called the Student Domestic Goods Year is to expect students to have special achievements in adopting domestic goods this year.

Half of the Student Domestic Goods Year has passed. Where are the achievements?

Students are the basic personnel of the country in the future, which no one can deny. If students cannot try their best to purchase domestic goods during the Student Domestic Goods Year, the future of the country is really chilling!

Leaving aside other things, let's just talk about paper, which is most closely related to our students. In the past, we used foreign paper for calculations and copying foreign texts. But now the exercise books produced by Tianzhang Paper Factory are very usable. The China National Products Company sells them for about 18 cents per dozen, which is much cheaper than foreign products. I usually use this kind of notebook for writing Chinese and Western texts or calculations, and I feel very at ease and happy because it is a domestic product. I really can't think of a good reason why we abandon usable domestic goods and use foreign goods. What is even more heartbreaking is that the intellectual class is still like this, let alone others?

How do we know that most of us are still using foreign goods? The most powerful evidence is that a domestic paper factory in Shanghai recently stopped production. Paper is considered to be the most closely related to students. Foreign paper is selling well and domestic paper factories are closing down during the Student Domestic Goods Year. This is the supreme shame for us students!

Domestic Silk

— Rong Yu

Due to the improvement of foreign silkworm breeding methods and the incentives for exported goods, our silk, which is known as a major export trade item, has almost no foothold in the world market. In addition, Chinese people love to wear imported woolen fabrics, and the continuous import of rayon has also caused domestic sales to plummet. If we don't think of ways to remedy this situation urgently, then not only will domestic silk disappear from the market, but there will also be no more mulberry planting and silkworm breeding in the countryside. Wouldn't this be another calamity for the production sector? Therefore, as citizens, although we cannot immediately regain the dominance of the silk industry, we should at least produce and use it ourselves to the greatest extent possible, and no longer allow imported woolen fabrics and silk fabrics to occupy their domestic position. Now, let's talk about the advantages of domestic silk so that people can consider it.

The so-called domestic silk naturally refers to that woven from silk. Anything woven from rayon or mixed with rayon is certainly not a qualified domestic product and cannot be called domestic. The advantages of domestic silk are that everyone knows it is strong, durable, and inexpensive. It is certainly more expensive than rayon, but much cheaper than pure silk fabrics from abroad. There are several scientific aspects: (1) Suitable for body weight. (2) Resistance to direct ultraviolet rays.

It is important to know that the ratio of clothing to body weight is also of great importance. Humans can keep warm and feel comfortable when wearing clothes that weigh one-tenth of their body weight. Of course, if the weight of the clothes is too great, there will be various losses, such as shortness of breath when walking, inconvenience in doing things, and easy congestion. The weight of silk is lighter than any clothing material (whether cotton weave, hemp weave, or wool weave), but its ability to keep out the cold is greater. A silk cotton robe weighing only two or three catties is warmer than an old sheepskin robe weighing seven or eight catties, which is clear evidence. Therefore, the lightness, warmth, and hygiene of domestic silk are unmatched by any clothing material.

Ultraviolet rays are very important for human health; however, according to hygienists, "Excessive absorption is as unpleasant as excessive sunbathing and is also harmful to health." Rayon and kapok are most able to pass ultraviolet rays, while natural silk has the greatest absorption rate. Therefore, we must also wear domestic silk to regulate the direct radiation of ultraviolet rays.

Okay! Since domestic silk has the above-mentioned advantages, fashionable people, hygienic people, and even economical people (because it is strong and easy to wash) might as well promote it more!

Introducing a Newly Emerging Shunchang Porcelain Factory

— Ru Yu

The development of China's porcelain industry has a very long history. Especially by the 13th century, its development not only reached its peak, but was also more powerful than that of any European country. For example, the famous German geographer Richthofen, who traveled in China for many years, left a book describing Chinese handicrafts very clearly. He said, "The technology of Chinese handicrafts has reached such a high level that every craftsman has his own automatic working machine, which is much higher than in Europe... Each department has a strict division of labor." Wok also said, "Each worker has his own special technology and his own special skills. One person paints birds, another paints flowers; one person adds red pigment, another adds blue color; counting up, until it is manufactured and sold, each piece of porcelain has to go through the hands of fifty workers."

The development of China's porcelain industry, the high level of technology, has reached this level, and it also has a very long history. In theory, China's porcelain industry should have the potential to develop by leaps and bounds and permanently hold the leading position in world porcelain production. However, turning to the customs trade booklets, not to mention other trade deficits, just looking at the annual import of porcelain alone, the number has reached an alarming figure and is increasing rather than decreasing. If this situation is not remedied urgently, the import of foreign porcelain cannot be stopped, and it will inevitably take over the original position of China's porcelain industry and squeeze the old Chinese porcelain industry out of the market. Looking at the trading situation of Jingdezhen porcelain, which is famous at home and abroad in recent years, it is not difficult to imagine its future. Therefore, improving China's porcelain industry at this time is a matter of urgency.

In the past, Shanghai had no manufacturing business of this kind, and it is really a pity and a pain to hand over such a good market to foreigners. Now, some people feel that this situation is getting more and more dangerous, so they set up a porcelain factory - Shunchang Porcelain Factory - at all costs to remedy it. Its scale is still in its initial stages, so it is not very large, there are very few workers, and the equipment is also very simple, but the raw materials used are all domestic products, and the porcelain styles are specially updated, and most of them are manufacturing the kind of foreign-style utensils that are imported from foreign countries. The progress of its future is naturally self-evident. This can be roughly understood by looking at the situation that orders from other factories are coming in one after another and they are too busy to handle them.

Shunchang Porcelain Factory has started to move forward in the face of this situation of promoting domestic goods and the flooding of foreign goods. It may also encounter obstacles in the middle. But I think that as long as the Chinese people adhere to their determination to supply and use domestic goods and persist in promoting domestic goods and rejecting foreign porcelain, not only can the Shunchang Porcelain Factory grow and develop, but also China's old porcelain industry will gradually improve. Therefore, I not only hope that Shunchang Porcelain Factory will work hard to improve and develop. I also hope that the Chinese people can unanimously maintain this industry that has just begun to blossom and bear fruit, so as to recover the lost rights and interests.
